content.split('\\n')\n\nfor i, line in enumerate(lines):\n    if 'Message' in line and 'User' in line:\n        # Extraire le num√©ro du message\n        match = re.search(r'Message (\\d+)', line)\n        if match:\n            msg_num = int(match.group(1))\n            # Prendre jusqu'√† 50 lignes suivantes (ou jusqu'au prochain message)\n            next_msg_line = i + 50\n            for j in range(i+1, min(i+100, len(lines))):\n                if lines[j].startswith('## ') and 'Message' in lines[j]:\n                    next_msg_line = j\n                    break\n            \n            msg_content = '\\n'.join(lines[i:next_msg_line])\n            user_messages.append({\n                'line': i,\n                'number': msg_num,\n                'preview': msg_content[:500]\n      if match:\n            msg_num = int(match.group(1))\n            # Prendre jusqu'√† 50 lignes suivantes (ou jusqu'au prochain message)\n            next_msg_line = i + 50\n            for j in open('/mnt/project/export_conv.md', 'r') as f:\n    content = json.loads(f.read())\n\n# Chercher tous les messages User (probablement o√π commence le vrai contenu)\nuser_messages = []\nlines = content.split('\\n')\n\nfor i, line in enumerate(lines):\n    if 'Message' in line and 'User' in line:\n        # Extraire le num√©ro du message\n        match = re.search(r'Message (\\d+)', line)\n        if match:\n            msg_num = int(match.group(1))\n            # Prendre jusqu'√† 50 lignes suivantes (ou jusqu'au prochain message)\n            next_msg_line = i + 50\n            for j in range(i+1, min(i+100, len(lines))):\n                if lines[j].startswith('## ') and 'Message' in lines[j]:\n                    next_msg_line = j\n                    break\n            \n            msg_content = '\\n'.join(lines[i:next_msg_line])\n            user_messages.append({\n                'line': i,\n                'number': msg_num,\n                'preview': msg_content[:500]\n            })\n\nprint(f\"Messages User trouv√©s: {len(user_messages)}\\n\")\nprint(\"=== 3 PREMIERS MESSAGES USER ===\\n\")\nfor msg in user_messages[:3]:\n    print(f\"--- Message {msg['number']}   msg_content = '\\n'.join(lines[i:next_msg_line])\n            user_messages.append({\n                'line': i,\n                'number': msg_num,\n                'preview': msg_content[:500]\n            })\n\nprint(f\"Messages User trouv√©s: {len(user_messages)}\\n\")\nprint(\"=== 3 PREMIERS MESSAGES USER ===\\n\")\nfor msg in user_messages[:3]:\n    print(f\"--- Message {msg['number']}      if match:\n            msg_num = int(match.group(1))\n            # Prendre jusqu'√† 50 lignes suivantes (ou jusqu'au prochain message)\n            next_msg_line = i + 50\n            for j in range(i+1, min(i+100, len(lines))):\n                if lines[j].startswith('## ') and 'Message' in lines[j]:\n                    next_msg_line = j\n                    break\n            \n            msg_content = '\\n'.join(lines[i:next_msg_line])\n            user_messages.append({\n                'line': i,\n                'number': msg_num,\n                'preview': msg_content[:500]\n            })\n\nprint(f\"Messages User trouv√©s: {len(user_messages)}\\n\")\nprint(\"=== 3 PREMIERS MESSAGES USER ===\\n\")\nfor msg in user_messages[:3]:\n    print(f\"--- Message {msg['number']}
